function MDXContent(props = {}) {
  const {wrapper: MDXLayout} = props.components || ({});
  return MDXLayout ? _jsx(MDXLayout, Object.assign({}, props, {
    children: _jsx(_createMdxContent, props)
  })) : _createMdxContent(props);
}

function MDXContent(props = {}) {
  const {wrapper: MDXLayout} = props.components || ({});
  return MDXLayout ? _jsx(MDXLayout, Object.assign({}, props, {
    children: _jsx(_createMdxContent, props)
  })) : _createMdxContent(props);
}
